moyi{
	fields(4){
		string	id('AB'), verb: false, required: true,type:id;
		string	name('Art0X艺术社区'), verb: false, required: true,type:string;
		string	description('艺术家、收藏家、艺术爱好者的交流天地'), verb: false, required: true,type:string;
		int	version('2147483647'), verb: false, required: true,type:version;
	}
	references field(105){
		moyiPlatformConfigurationList	moyi(全局配置)--moyi;
		moyiPlatformConfigurationV2List	moyi(全局配置)--moyi;
		survivalStatusList	moyi(社区治理)--moyi;
		slideList	moyi(App展示管理)--moyi;
		slideTypeList	moyi(App展示管理)--moyi;
		channelList	moyi(App展示管理)--moyi;
		channelTypeList	moyi(App展示管理)--moyi;
		channelSectionTypeList	moyi(App展示管理)--moyi;
		channelSectionList	moyi(App展示管理)--moyi;
		masterColumnList	moyi(App展示管理)--moyi;
